< Review>
Sadly when I needed some help I was told NO. I happen to be laying over in Kerman for a couple months because I didn't like what I seen in Fresno. I am a full time RVer working as a camp host or doing maintenance. The phone I just received stopped working and the company wouldn't send it general delivery to the post office. So I needed an address I could have it sent to. I thought why not ask if the local church could help. So I stopped in and ask if they could receive a package a replacement phone. They said they would have to ask the father and would get back to me by 4pm. Well after not receiving a message I thought I would stop by the next morning. I went in and asked if it was ok I was told NO they wouldn't. So I said I guess I'll have to find a church that could help out...... How sad it is when you can't get help from the church when you really need it...........I did find a local church that had no problem accepting my package. So while staying in Kerman I went to The Fathers House every Sunday after that...!!!< /Review>

I live right next to this market and feel so fortunate to have Franklin Bros. It's far from your average corner store. I often go twice a day- to get a fresh coffee and pastry in the morning and again for Acme bread, veggies or wine in the evening. Even though the prices are great, I probably spend way too much money there, but I don't even care because the people are so nice. They know my name (along with many neighborhood faces) and have even let me borrow a tape measure when I needed it. It feels good to give money to a place that is supporting a healthy community. I wish every neighborhood could have a Franklin Bros Market. Thank you for providing an amazing place for us!</text>

< Review>
I have had issues with mechanics in the past (talking down to me because I'm a woman even though I know a decent amount about cars). But I found Firestone and I couldn't be happier. I've been taking my car here for years now and have always had a positive experience, fair pricing, and zero condescension.
I've noticed they treat all their customers with respect. Sitting in the waiting room, you can hear them tell customers "here's the urgent items, and here's the items we recommend but if you wait, won't leave you on the side of the road."
I recommend this shop to anyone looking for an honest and fairly priced mechanic.</Review>
